<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leggen.html>leggen</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:leggen.html>leggen</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lagjaną</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:legio.html>legio</a> (69067)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">legiō</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:after.html>after</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:story.html>story</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:legio.html>Legio</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> demoniac. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> neuter gender <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>noun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a> “multitude” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> influenced <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:related.html>related</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:term.html>term</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:legioen.html>legioen</a></i>. <hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:leiden.html>leiden</a></b> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leidster.html>leidster</a> (30429)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***lekken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lekken.html>lekken</a> (10821)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:lekken.html>lekken</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lakjaną</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a> (370)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lecker</i>, derived <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>verb</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekken.html>lekken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:lick.html>lick</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:likken.html>likken</a></i>). Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">lecker</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Afrikaans" class="extiw" title="w:Afrikaans"><a href = vnd.unilang:afrikaans.html>Afrikaans</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">lecker</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">läcker</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">lækker</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:more.html>More</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lick.html>lick</a>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekken.html>lekken</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekkers.html>lekkers</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekkertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p>Calque <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a>  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">līlium</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a>  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Translingualism" class="extiw" title="w:Translingualism">translingual</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="mul">Convallaria</i>. Literally, “little <a href = vnd.unilang:lily.html>lily</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> [<a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a>] dales”.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:lily.html>lily</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:valley.html>valley</a> (<i>Convallaria majalis</i>)</li></ol>
